<p>The <b>Wikimedia Foundation</b> (<b>WMF</b>) is an American non-profit and <a href="/wiki/Foundation_(nonprofit)" title="Foundation (nonprofit)">charitable organization</a> headquartered in <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">San Francisco</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>, that operates many <a href="/wiki/Wiki" title="Wiki">wikis</a>. The foundation is mostly known for hosting <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Internet_encyclopedia" title="Internet encyclopedia" class="mw-redirect">Internet encyclopedia</a>, as well as <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary" title="Wiktionary">Wiktionary</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikiquote" title="Wikiquote">Wikiquote</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikibooks" title="Wikibooks">Wikibooks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikisource" title="Wikisource">Wikisource</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_Commons" title="Wikimedia Commons">Wikimedia Commons</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikispecies" title="Wikispecies">Wikispecies</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikinews" title="Wikinews">Wikinews</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikiversity" title="Wikiversity">Wikiversity</a>, <a href="/wiki/WikiData" title="WikiData" class="mw-redirect">WikiData</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wikivoyage" title="Wikivoyage">Wikivoyage</a>, Wikimedia Incubator, and <a href="//meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Main_Page" class="extiw" title="m:Main Page">Meta-Wiki</a>. It also owned the now-defunct <a href="/wiki/Nupedia" title="Nupedia">Nupedia</a>.</p>
<p>The organization was founded in 2003 by <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Wales" title="Jimmy Wales">Jimmy Wales</a>, co-founder of Wikipedia, as a way to fund Wikipedia and its sister projects through non-profit means.<sup id="cite_ref-Rupert_Neate_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rupert_Neate-5"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Announcing_Wikimedia_Foundation_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Announcing_Wikimedia_Foundation-6"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>As of 2015<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, the foundation employs around 250 people, with annual revenues in excess of US$50 million.<sup id="cite_ref-2013-2014_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013-2014-7"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Lila_Tretikov" title="Lila Tretikov">Lila Tretikov</a> leads the foundation as its <a href="/wiki/Executive_director" title="Executive director">executive director</a>, and Patricio Lorente is <a href="/wiki/Chairman_of_the_board" title="Chairman of the board" class="mw-redirect">chairman of the board</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Goal">Goal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Goal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Wikimedia Foundation falls under section <a href="/wiki/501(c)#501.28c.29.283.29" title="501(c)" class="mw-redirect">501(c)(3)</a> of the US <a href="/wiki/Internal_Revenue_Code" title="Internal Revenue Code">Internal Revenue Code</a> as a <a href="/wiki/Charitable_organization" title="Charitable organization">public charity</a>. Its <a href="/wiki/National_Taxonomy_of_Exempt_Entities" title="National Taxonomy of Exempt Entities">National Taxonomy of Exempt Entities</a> (NTEE) code is B60 (<a href="/wiki/Adult_education" title="Adult education">Adult</a>, <a href="/wiki/Continuing_education" title="Continuing education">Continuing education</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup> The foundation's by-laws declare a statement of purpose of collecting and developing educational content and to disseminate it effectively and globally.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10"><span>[</span>10<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>The Wikimedia Foundation's stated goal is to develop and maintain <a href="/wiki/Open_content" title="Open content">open content</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wiki" title="Wiki">wiki</a>-based projects and to provide the full contents of those projects to the public <a href="/wiki/Gratis" title="Gratis">free of charge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-wikimedia-mission_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wikimedia-mission-11"><span>[</span>11<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In 2001, <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Wales" title="Jimmy Wales">Jimmy Wales</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Internet_entrepreneur" title="Internet entrepreneur" class="mw-redirect">Internet entrepreneur</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Larry_Sanger" title="Larry Sanger">Larry Sanger</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Software_developer" title="Software developer">software developer</a>, founded Wikipedia, an Internet encyclopedia. The project was originally funded by <a href="/wiki/Bomis" title="Bomis">Bomis</a>, Wales' for-profit business. As Wikipedia's popularity skyrocketed, revenues to fund the project stalled.<sup id="cite_ref-Rupert_Neate_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rupert_Neate-5"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup> Since Wikipedia was depleting Bomis' resources, Wales and <a href="/wiki/Larry_Sanger" title="Larry Sanger">Sanger</a> thought of a charity model to fund the project.<sup id="cite_ref-Rupert_Neate_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Rupert_Neate-5"><span>[</span>5<span>]</span></a></sup> The Wikimedia Foundation was then created from Wikipedia and <a href="/wiki/Nupedia" title="Nupedia">Nupedia</a> on June 20, 2003.<sup id="cite_ref-Announcing_Wikimedia_Foundation_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Announcing_Wikimedia_Foundation-6"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup> It applied to the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Patent_and_Trademark_Office" title="United States Patent and Trademark Office">United States Patent and Trademark Office</a> to trademark <i>Wikipedia</i> on September 17, 2004. The mark was granted registration status on January 10, 2006. Trademark protection was accorded by Japan on December 16, 2004, and, in the European Union, on January 20, 2005. There were plans to license the use of the Wikipedia trademark for some products, such as books or DVDs.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span>[</span>12<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In April 2005, the US <a href="/wiki/Internal_Revenue_Service" title="Internal Revenue Service">Internal Revenue Service</a> approved the foundation as an educational foundation in the category "<a href="/wiki/Adult_education" title="Adult education">Adult</a>, <a href="/wiki/Continuing_education" title="Continuing education">Continuing education</a>", meaning all contributions to the foundation are <a href="/wiki/Tax_deduction" title="Tax deduction">tax-deductible</a> for US federal income tax purposes.</p>
<p>On December 11, 2006, the Foundation's board noted that the corporation could not become the <a href="/wiki/Cooperative" title="Cooperative">membership organization</a> initially planned but never implemented due to an inability to meet the registration requirements of Florida statutory law. Accordingly, the by-laws were amended to remove all reference to membership rights and activities. The decision to change the bylaws was passed by the board unanimously.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On September 25, 2007, the foundation's board gave notice that the operations would be moving to the <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_Bay_Area" title="San Francisco Bay Area">San Francisco Bay Area</a>. Major considerations cited for choosing San Francisco were proximity to like-minded organizations and potential partners, a better talent pool, as well as cheaper and more convenient international travel than is available from <a href="/wiki/St._Petersburg,_Florida" title="St. Petersburg, Florida">St. Petersburg, Florida</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-MoncadaWikimoveTribune_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MoncadaWikimoveTribune-14"><span>[</span>14<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MullinsWikimoveTribune_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MullinsWikimoveTribune-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-KimWikimoveSFChronicle_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-KimWikimoveSFChronicle-16"><span>[</span>16<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Projects_and_initiatives">Projects and initiatives</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Projects and initiatives">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wikimedia_projects"><span id="Projects"></span> Wikimedia projects</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Wikimedia projects">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_projects" title="Wikimedia projects" class="mw-redirect">Wikimedia projects</a></div>
<p>In addition to Wikipedia, the foundation operates other wikis that follow the <a href="/wiki/Free_content" title="Free content">free content</a> model with their main goal being the dissemination of knowledge. These include:</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chapters">Chapters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Chapters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia_chapters.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Wikimedia_chapters.svg/220px-Wikimedia_chapters.svg.png" width="220" height="112" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Wikimedia_chapters.svg/330px-Wikimedia_chapters.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Wikimedia_chapters.svg/440px-Wikimedia_chapters.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1410" data-file-height="715" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia_chapters.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
(<span style="color:#008"><b>dark blue</b></span>) are existing chapters. (<span style="color:#068"><b>dark turquoise</b></span>) indicates a chapter has been board approved but not yet founded. (<span style="color:#0a8"><b>green</b></span>) indicates a chapter is in the planning stages. (<span style="color:#0dd"><b>light blue</b></span>) indicates a chapter in discussion.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_Wikimedia_chapters" title="List of Wikimedia chapters">List of Wikimedia chapters</a></div>
<p><a href="//meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_chapters" class="extiw" title="m:Wikimedia chapters">Wikimedia chapters</a> are national (or in some cases sub-national) not-for-profit organisations created to support and promote the Wikimedia projects locally.<sup id="cite_ref-MetaChap_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MetaChap-17"><span>[</span>17<span>]</span></a></sup> The chapters are independent of the Wikimedia Foundation, with no legal control of nor responsibility for the Wikimedia projects. The organizations are recognized and overseen by a <a href="//meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Chapters_Committee" class="extiw" title="m:Chapters Committee">Chapters Committee</a>; following approval they enter into a "Chapters Agreement" with the foundation.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18"><span>[</span>18<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup> As of April 2012<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, there were 39 recognized Wikimedia chapters.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20"><span>[</span>20<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wikimania">Wikimania</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Wikimania">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Wikimania" title="Wikimania">Wikimania</a></div>
<p>Each year, an international conference called Wikimania brings the people together who are involved in the Wikimedia organizations and projects. The first Wikimania was held in <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt" title="Frankfurt">Frankfurt</a>, Germany, in 2005. Nowadays, Wikimania is organized by a committee supported usually by the national chapter, in collaboration with the Wikimedia Foundation. Wikimania has been held in cities such as <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-2009-website_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2009-website-21"><span>[</span>21<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Cambridge,_Massachusetts" title="Cambridge, Massachusetts">Cambridge</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-attendees2006_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-attendees2006-22"><span>[</span>22<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Haifa" title="Haifa">Haifa</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-themarker_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-themarker-23"><span>[</span>23<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24"><span>[</span>24<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25"><span>[</span>25<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2015, Wikimania took place in <a href="/wiki/Mexico_City" title="Mexico City">Mexico City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2016, Wikimania will be held in <a href="/wiki/Esino_Lario" title="Esino Lario">Esino Lario</a>, <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27"><span>[</span>27<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Strategic_plan">Strategic plan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Strategic plan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lila_Tretikov_April_2014_(5)_crop.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Lila_Tretikov_April_2014_%285%29_crop.jpg/220px-Lila_Tretikov_April_2014_%285%29_crop.jpg" width="220" height="270" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Lila_Tretikov_April_2014_%285%29_crop.jpg/330px-Lila_Tretikov_April_2014_%285%29_crop.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Lila_Tretikov_April_2014_%285%29_crop.jpg/440px-Lila_Tretikov_April_2014_%285%29_crop.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3046" data-file-height="3736" /></a>

Executive director <a href="/wiki/Lila_Tretikov" title="Lila Tretikov">Lila Tretikov</a>, 2014</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In response to the growing size and popularity of Wikipedia, the Wikimedia Foundation announced a Strategic Plan to improve and sustain the Wikimedia movement. The plan was announced in July 2009, followed by a process of interviews and surveys with people from across the Wikimedia movement, including board of trustees, members of staff and volunteer editors.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span>[</span>28<span>]</span></a></sup> The ongoing plan was intended to be the basis of a five-year plan to further outreach, improve content quality and quality control, and optimising operational areas such as finance and infrastructure.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span>[</span>29<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wikipedia_Usability_Initiative">Wikipedia Usability Initiative</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Wikipedia Usability Initiative">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In December 2008, the Wikimedia Foundation announced a restricted donation grant of $890,000 from the <a href="/wiki/Stanton_Foundation" title="Stanton Foundation">Stanton Foundation</a>, to improve Wikipedia's accessibility.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span>[</span>30<span>]</span></a></sup> Later named the Wikipedia Usability Initiative, the grant was used by the Wikimedia Foundation to appoint project-specific staff to the technology department.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span>[</span>31<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>A series of surveys were conducted throughout 2009. This began with a qualitative environment survey on <a href="/wiki/MediaWiki" title="MediaWiki">MediaWiki</a> extensions, followed by a Qualitative Statistical Survey focusing on volume of edits, number of new users, and related statistics. In March 2009, a usability and experience study was carried out on new and non-editors of the English Wikipedia. The aim was to discover what obstacles participants encountered while editing Wikipedia, ranging from small changes to more complicated syntax such as templates. The study recruited 2500 people for in-person laboratory testing via the Wikipedia website, which was filtered down to ten participants. The results were collated and used by the technology team to improve Wikipedia's usability.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span>[</span>32<span>]</span></a></sup> The Usability and Experience Study was followed up by the Usability, Experience and Progress Study in September 2009. This study recruited different new and non-editors for in-person trials on a new Wikipedia skin.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33"><span>[</span>33<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>The initiative ultimately culminated in a new Wikipedia skin named Vector, constructed based on the results of the usability studies. This was introduced by default in stages, beginning in May 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34"><span>[</span>34<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Public_Policy_Initiative">Public Policy Initiative</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Public Policy Initiative">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In May 2010, the Wikimedia Foundation announced the Public Policy Initiative, following a $1.2 million donation by the Stanton Foundation. The Initiative was set up to improve articles relating to public policy–related issues.<sup id="cite_ref-pubpol_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pubpol-35"><span>[</span>35<span>]</span></a></sup> As part of the initiative, Wikipedia collaborated with ten universities to help students and professors create and maintain articles relating to public policy.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36"><span>[</span>36<span>]</span></a></sup> Volunteer editors of Wikipedia, known as "ambassadors", provided assistance to students and professors. This was either done on campus sites or online.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37"><span>[</span>37<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Technology">Technology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Technology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The foundation employs technology including hardware and software to run its projects.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hardware">Hardware</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Hardware">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="metadata plainlinks ambox ambox-content ambox-Update" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image">
<div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_current_red.svg" class="image"><img alt="Ambox current red.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/42px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png" width="42" height="34" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/63px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/84px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="360" data-file-height="290" /></a></div>
</td>
<td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">This section is <b>outdated</b>. <span class="hide-when-compact">Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.</span> <small><i>(August 2014)</i></small></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia-servers-2010-12-28.svg" class="image"><img alt="Diagram showing flow of data between Wikipedia's servers. Twenty database servers talk to hundreds of Apache servers in the backend; Apaches talk to fifty squids in the frontend." src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Wikimedia-servers-2010-12-28.svg/220px-Wikimedia-servers-2010-12-28.svg.png" width="220" height="237" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Wikimedia-servers-2010-12-28.svg/330px-Wikimedia-servers-2010-12-28.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Wikimedia-servers-2010-12-28.svg/440px-Wikimedia-servers-2010-12-28.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="1290" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia-servers-2010-12-28.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Overview of system architecture, December 2010. See <a href="//meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Server_layout_diagrams" class="extiw" title="meta:Server layout diagrams">server layout diagrams on Meta-Wiki</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia_Foundation_Servers-8055_13.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Wikimedia_Foundation_Servers-8055_13.jpg/220px-Wikimedia_Foundation_Servers-8055_13.jpg" width="220" height="94" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Wikimedia_Foundation_Servers-8055_13.jpg/330px-Wikimedia_Foundation_Servers-8055_13.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/94/Wikimedia_Foundation_Servers-8055_13.jpg/440px-Wikimedia_Foundation_Servers-8055_13.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5184" data-file-height="2206" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia_Foundation_Servers-8055_13.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Wikimedia Foundation servers</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Wikimedia currently runs on dedicated <a href="/wiki/Cluster_(computing)" title="Cluster (computing)" class="mw-redirect">clusters</a> of <a href="/wiki/Linux" title="Linux">Linux</a> servers (mainly <a href="/wiki/Ubuntu_(operating_system)" title="Ubuntu (operating system)">Ubuntu</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38"><span>[</span>38<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup> As of December 2009<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, there were 300 in Florida and 44 in <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-servers_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-servers-40"><span>[</span>40<span>]</span></a></sup> Wikipedia employed a single server until 2004, when the server setup was expanded into a distributed <a href="/wiki/Multitier_architecture" title="Multitier architecture">multitier architecture</a>. In January 2005, the project ran on 39 <a href="/wiki/Dedicated_hosting_service" title="Dedicated hosting service">dedicated servers</a> in Florida.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2014)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> This configuration included a single master <a href="/wiki/Database_server" title="Database server">database server</a> running <a href="/wiki/MySQL" title="MySQL">MySQL</a>, multiple slave database servers, 21 <a href="/wiki/Web_server" title="Web server">web servers</a> running the <a href="/wiki/Apache_HTTP_Server" title="Apache HTTP Server">Apache HTTP Server</a>, and seven <a href="/wiki/Squid_(software)" title="Squid (software)">Squid cache</a> servers.</p>
<p>Wikipedia receives between 25,000 and 60,000-page requests per second, depending on the time of day.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41"><span>[</span>41<span>]</span></a></sup> Page requests are first passed to a front-end layer of Squid-caching servers.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42"><span>[</span>42<span>]</span></a></sup> Further statistics are available based on a publicly available 3-months Wikipedia access trace.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43"><span>[</span>43<span>]</span></a></sup> Requests that cannot be served from the Squid cache are sent to load-balancing servers running the <a href="/wiki/Linux_Virtual_Server" title="Linux Virtual Server">Linux Virtual Server</a> software, which in turn pass the request to one of the Apache web servers for page rendering from the database. The web servers deliver pages as requested, performing page rendering for all the language editions of Wikipedia. To increase speed further, rendered pages are cached in a distributed memory cache until invalidated, allowing page rendering to be skipped entirely for most common page accesses.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Softw.D0.B0r.D0.B5">Softwаrе</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Softwаrе">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote">See also: <a href="/wiki/MediaWiki" title="MediaWiki">MediaWiki</a> and <a href="/wiki/VisualEditor" title="VisualEditor">VisualEditor</a></div>
<p>The operation of Wikimedia depends on <a href="/wiki/MediaWiki" title="MediaWiki">MediaWiki</a>, a custom-made, <a href="/wiki/Free_software" title="Free software">free</a> and <a href="/wiki/Open-source_software" title="Open-source software">open-source</a> <a href="/wiki/Wiki_software" title="Wiki software">wiki software</a> platform written in <a href="/wiki/PHP" title="PHP">PHP</a> and built upon the <a href="/wiki/MySQL" title="MySQL">MySQL</a> database.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44"><span>[</span>44<span>]</span></a></sup> The software incorporates programming features such as a <a href="/wiki/Macro_(computer_science)" title="Macro (computer science)">macro language</a>, <a href="/wiki/Variable_(programming)" title="Variable (programming)" class="mw-redirect">variables</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Transclusion" title="Transclusion">transclusion</a> system for <a href="/wiki/Web_template" title="Web template" class="mw-redirect">templates</a>, and <a href="/wiki/URL_redirection" title="URL redirection">URL redirection</a>. MediaWiki is licensed under the <a href="/wiki/GNU_General_Public_License" title="GNU General Public License">GNU General Public License</a> and it is used by all Wikimedia projects, as well as many other wiki projects. Originally, Wikipedia ran on <a href="/wiki/UseModWiki" title="UseModWiki">UseModWiki</a> written in <a href="/wiki/Perl" title="Perl">Perl</a> by Clifford Adams (Phase I), which initially required <a href="/wiki/CamelCase" title="CamelCase">CamelCase</a> for article hyperlinks; the present double bracket style was incorporated later. Starting in January 2002 (Phase II), Wikipedia began running on a <a href="/wiki/PhpWiki" title="PhpWiki">PHP wiki</a> engine with a MySQL database; this software was custom-made for Wikipedia by <a href="/wiki/Magnus_Manske" title="Magnus Manske">Magnus Manske</a>. The Phase II software was repeatedly modified to accommodate the <a href="/wiki/Exponential_growth" title="Exponential growth">exponentially increasing</a> demand. In July 2002 (Phase III), Wikipedia shifted to the third-generation software, MediaWiki, originally written by <a href="/wiki/Lee_Daniel_Crocker" title="Lee Daniel Crocker">Lee Daniel Crocker</a>. Several MediaWiki extensions are <a href="/wiki/Special:Version#Installed_extensions" title="Special:Version">installed</a> to extend the functionality of MediaWiki software. In April 2005, a <a href="/wiki/Lucene" title="Lucene">Lucene</a> extension<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45"><span>[</span>45<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46"><span>[</span>46<span>]</span></a></sup> was added to MediaWiki's built-in search and Wikipedia switched from <a href="/wiki/MySQL" title="MySQL">MySQL</a> to Lucene for searching. Currently Lucene Search 2.1,<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup> which is written in <a href="/wiki/Java_(programming_language)" title="Java (programming language)">Java</a> and based on Lucene library 2.3,<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48"><span>[</span>48<span>]</span></a></sup> is used. Wikimedia Foundation also uses <a href="/wiki/CiviCRM" title="CiviCRM">CiviCRM</a><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49"><span>[</span>49<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/WordPress" title="WordPress">WordPress</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50"><span>[</span>50<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>The Foundation published official Wikipedia <a href="/wiki/Mobile_apps" title="Mobile apps" class="mw-redirect">mobile apps</a> for <a href="/wiki/Android_(operating_system)" title="Android (operating system)">Android</a> and <a href="/wiki/IOS" title="IOS">iOS</a> devices and in March 2015, the apps were updated to include mobile user friendly features.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51"><span>[</span>51<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Finances">Finances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Finances">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="In_general">In general</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: In general">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote">See also: <a href="//wikimediafoundation.org/wiki/Financial_reports" class="extiw" title="wmf:Financial reports">wmf:Financial reports</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia_Foundation_financial_development_2003-2012.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Wikimedia_Foundation_financial_development_2003-2012.png/220px-Wikimedia_Foundation_financial_development_2003-2012.png" width="220" height="222" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Wikimedia_Foundation_financial_development_2003-2012.png/330px-Wikimedia_Foundation_financial_development_2003-2012.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/2/24/Wikimedia_Foundation_financial_development_2003-2012.png 2x" data-file-width="423" data-file-height="426" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia_Foundation_financial_development_2003-2012.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Financial development of the Wikimedia Foundation, 2003–2013
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:green; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Support and Revenue</div>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:red; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Expenses</div>
<div class="legend"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:black; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Net assets at year-end</div>
Wikimedia Foundation, Inc. Financial Statements</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The Wikimedia Foundation relies on public contributions and grants to fund its mission.<sup id="cite_ref-financialstatements_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-financialstatements-52"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup> It is exempt from federal income tax<sup id="cite_ref-financialstatements_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-financialstatements-52"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53"><span>[</span>53<span>]</span></a></sup> and from state income tax.<sup id="cite_ref-financialstatements_52-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-financialstatements-52"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54"><span>[</span>54<span>]</span></a></sup> It is not a private foundation, and contributions to it qualify as tax-deductible charitable contributions.<sup id="cite_ref-financialstatements_52-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-financialstatements-52"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>The continued technical and economic growth of each of the Wikimedia projects is dependent mostly on donations but the Wikimedia Foundation also increases its revenue by alternative means of funding such as <a href="/wiki/Federal_grant" title="Federal grant" class="mw-redirect">grants</a>, sponsorship, services and brand merchandising. The Wikimedia <a href="/wiki/OAI-PMH" title="OAI-PMH" class="mw-redirect">OAI-PMH</a> update feed service, targeted primarily at search engines and similar bulk analysis and republishing, has been a source of revenue for several years,<sup id="cite_ref-financialstatements_52-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-financialstatements-52"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup> but is no longer open to new customers.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55"><span>[</span>55<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/DBpedia" title="DBpedia">DBpedia</a> was given access to this feed free of charge.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup> In July 2014, the Foundation announced it would be accepting <a href="/wiki/Bitcoin" title="Bitcoin">Bitcoin</a> donations.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57"><span>[</span>57<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Since the end of fiscal year ended 2004, the Foundation's net assets have grown from $57K<sup id="cite_ref-financialstatements2006_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-financialstatements2006-58"><span>[</span>58<span>]</span></a></sup> to $53.5M at the end of fiscal year ended June 30, 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-2013-2014_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2013-2014-7"><span>[</span>7<span>]</span></a></sup> Under the leadership of Sue Gardner, who joined the Wikimedia Foundation in 2007, the Foundation's staff levels, number of donors and revenue have seen very significant growth.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59"><span>[</span>59<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">

Interview with Garfield Byrd, Chief of Finance and Administration at the Wikimedia Foundation. Recorded October 7, 2011</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In 2007, <a href="/wiki/Charity_Navigator" title="Charity Navigator">Charity Navigator</a> gave Wikimedia an overall rating of three out of four possible stars<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60"><span>[</span>60<span>]</span></a></sup> (one out of four in efficiency, which has been criticised).<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61"><span>[</span>61<span>]</span></a></sup> Charity Navigator gave three out of four possible stars in overall rating for fiscal years 2008 and 2009 which improved to four-stars in 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62"><span>[</span>62<span>]</span></a></sup> The current overall rating is four stars – three stars for Financial, four stars for Accountability and Transparency.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63"><span>[</span>63<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>There are both supporting and opposing arguments regarding whether Wikimedia should switch to an advertising-based revenue model.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64"><span>[</span>64<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Grants">Grants</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Grants">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Finance_Meeting_Paris_2012-02-18_n06.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Finance_Meeting_Paris_2012-02-18_n06.jpg/220px-Finance_Meeting_Paris_2012-02-18_n06.jpg" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Finance_Meeting_Paris_2012-02-18_n06.jpg/330px-Finance_Meeting_Paris_2012-02-18_n06.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Finance_Meeting_Paris_2012-02-18_n06.jpg/440px-Finance_Meeting_Paris_2012-02-18_n06.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3000" data-file-height="1993" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Finance_Meeting_Paris_2012-02-18_n06.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Wikimedia Foundation and chapters finance meeting 2012, Paris</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In March 2008, the Foundation announced a large donation, at the time its largest donation yet: a three-year, $3 million grant from the <a href="/wiki/Alfred_P._Sloan_Foundation" title="Alfred P. Sloan Foundation">Alfred P. Sloan Foundation</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-3mill_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3mill-65"><span>[</span>65<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In 2009, the Foundation received four grants&#160;– the first grant was a $890,000 <a href="/wiki/Frank_Stanton_(executive)" title="Frank Stanton (executive)">Stanton Foundation</a> grant which was aimed to help study and simplify user interface for first-time authors of Wikipedia.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66"><span>[</span>66<span>]</span></a></sup> The second was a $300,000 <a href="/wiki/Ford_Foundation" title="Ford Foundation">Ford Foundation</a> Grant, given in July 2009, for <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_Commons" title="Wikimedia Commons">Wikimedia Commons</a> that aimed to improve the interfaces and workflows for multimedia uploading on Wikimedia websites.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67"><span>[</span>67<span>]</span></a></sup> In August 2009, the Foundation received a $500,000 grant from The William and Flora <a href="/wiki/Hewlett_Foundation" title="Hewlett Foundation" class="mw-redirect">Hewlett Foundation</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span>[</span>68<span>]</span></a></sup> Lastly, in August 2009, the <a href="/wiki/Omidyar_Network" title="Omidyar Network">Omidyar Network</a> issued a potential<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (August 2015)">clarification needed</span></a></i>]</sup> $2 million in "grant" funding to Wikimedia.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69"><span>[</span>69<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In 2010, the <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a> corporation donated $2 million to the Foundation.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70"><span>[</span>70<span>]</span></a></sup> Also in 2010, the William and Flora Hewlett Foundation pledged a $800,000 grant and all was funded during 2011.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>In March 2011, the Alfred P. Sloan Foundation authorized another $3 million grant to continue to develop and maintain the Foundation's mission. The grant was to be funded over three years with the first $1 million funded in July 2011 and the remaining $2 million was scheduled to be funded in August 2012 and 2013. In August 2011, the Stanton Foundation pledged to fund a $3.6 million grant of which $1.8 million was funded and the remaining was due to be funded in September 2012. As of 2011, this was the largest grant received by the Wikimedia Foundation to-date.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71"><span>[</span>71<span>]</span></a></sup> In November 2011, the Foundation received a $500,000 donation from Google co-founder <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Brin" title="Sergey Brin">Sergey Brin</a> and his wife.<sup id="cite_ref-foundationgrants_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-foundationgrants-72"><span>[</span>72<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73"><span>[</span>73<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In 2012, the Foundation was awarded a grant of $1.25 million from the historians <a href="/wiki/Lisbet_Rausing" title="Lisbet Rausing">Lisbet Rausing</a><sup id="cite_ref-foundationgrants_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-foundationgrants-72"><span>[</span>72<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Baldwin_(professor)" title="Peter Baldwin (professor)">Peter Baldwin</a> through <a href="/wiki/Charities_Aid_Foundation" title="Charities Aid Foundation">Charities Aid Foundation</a>, scheduled to be funded in five equal installments. The first installment of $250,000 was received in April 2012 and the remaining were to be funded in December 2012 through 2015.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Financial_summary">Financial summary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Financial summary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Governance">Governance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Governance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Board_of_Trustees">Board of Trustees</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Board of Trustees">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Patricio_Lorente.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Patricio_Lorente.jpg/220px-Patricio_Lorente.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Patricio_Lorente.jpg/330px-Patricio_Lorente.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Patricio_Lorente.jpg/440px-Patricio_Lorente.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4598" data-file-height="3065" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Patricio_Lorente.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Patricio Lorente, the current Chairman of the Board</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Board_of_trustees" title="Board of trustees" class="mw-redirect">board of trustees</a> has ultimate authority of all the businesses and affairs of the Foundation. It is composed of ten members:</p>
<ul>
<li>four who are appointed by the Board itself;</li>
<li>three who are selected by the community encompassed by all the different Wikimedia projects;</li>
<li>two who are selected by the local chapters and thematic organizations;</li>
<li>and one <a href="/wiki/Emeritus" title="Emeritus">emeritus</a> for the foundation's founder, <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Wales" title="Jimmy Wales">Jimmy Wales</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-April2008_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-April2008-82"><span>[</span>82<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<p>Three permanent entities support the board on its mission and responsibilities: an executive director, namely <a href="/wiki/Lila_Tretikov" title="Lila Tretikov">Lila Tretikov</a>, which leads and oversees the operational arm of the foundation; an advisory board composed of individuals selected by the board itself that advise the board on different matters; and <a href="/wiki/Standing_committee" title="Standing committee" class="mw-redirect">standing committees</a> to which the board delegates certain matters while retaining ultimate authority. The board has also at times created other orthodox entities<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Please_clarify" title="Wikipedia:Please clarify"><span title="The text near this tag may need clarification or removal of jargon. (July 2015)">clarification needed</span></a></i>]</sup> to support itself, such as <a href="/wiki/Executive_secretary" title="Executive secretary" class="mw-redirect">executive secretaries</a> and ad-hoc committees established for specific tasks.</p>
<p>The current board comprises Patricio Lorente as Chairman and Alice Wiegand as Vice-Chairman, together with Frieda Brioschi, <a href="/wiki/James_Heilman" title="James Heilman">James Heilman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dariusz_Jemielniak" title="Dariusz Jemielniak">Dariusz Jemielniak</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guy_Kawasaki" title="Guy Kawasaki">Guy Kawasaki</a>, Denny Vrandečić, Jan-Bart de Vreede, <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Wales" title="Jimmy Wales">Jimmy Wales</a> and Stu West as members at-large.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Advisory_board">Advisory board</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Advisory board">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Advisory Board, according to the Wikimedia Foundation, is an international network of experts who have agreed to give the foundation meaningful help on a regular basis in many different areas, including law, organizational development, technology, policy, and outreach.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83"><span>[</span>83<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Staff">Staff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Staff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="First_appointments">First appointments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: First appointments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

Staff and workplace at Wikimedia Foundation's <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">San Francisco</a> office</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In 2004, the foundation appointed Tim Starling as developer liaison to help improve the <a href="/wiki/MediaWiki" title="MediaWiki">MediaWiki</a> software, Daniel Mayer as chief financial officer (<a href="/wiki/Management_accounting" title="Management accounting">finance</a>, <a href="/wiki/Budgeting" title="Budgeting" class="mw-redirect">budgeting</a>, and coordination of fund drives), and <a href="/wiki/Erik_M%C3%B6ller" title="Erik Möller">Erik Möller</a> as content partnership coordinator. In May 2005, the foundation announced seven more official appointments.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84"><span>[</span>84<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template noprint Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTRS" title="Wikipedia:NOTRS" class="mw-redirect"><span title="This claim needs references to better sources. (July 2014)">better&#160;source&#160;needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<p>In January 2006, the foundation created several committees, including the Communication Committee, in an attempt to further organize activities essentially handled by volunteers at that time.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85"><span>[</span>85<span>]</span></a></sup> Starling resigned that month to spend more time on his PhD program.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Employees">Employees</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Employees">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia_Foundation_Office_Officey_Photos-5.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Wikimedia_Foundation_Office_Officey_Photos-5.jpg/220px-Wikimedia_Foundation_Office_Officey_Photos-5.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Wikimedia_Foundation_Office_Officey_Photos-5.jpg/330px-Wikimedia_Foundation_Office_Officey_Photos-5.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Wikimedia_Foundation_Office_Officey_Photos-5.jpg/440px-Wikimedia_Foundation_Office_Officey_Photos-5.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4984" data-file-height="3322" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Wikimedia_Foundation_Office_Officey_Photos-5.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A workers area at the Wikimedia Foundation's San Francisco headquarters</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The foundation's functions were, for the first few years, executed almost entirely by volunteers. In 2005, it had only two employees, Danny Wool, a coordinator, and Brion Vibber, a software manager.</p>
<p>As of October 4, 2006<sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit">[update]</a></sup>, the foundation had five paid employees:<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86"><span>[</span>86<span>]</span></a></sup> two programmers, an administrative assistant, a coordinator handling fundraising and grants, and an interim <a href="/wiki/Chief_executive_officer" title="Chief executive officer">executive director</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87"><span>[</span>87<span>]</span></a></sup> Brad Patrick, previously the foundation's <a href="/wiki/General_counsel" title="General counsel">general counsel</a>. Patrick ceased his activity as interim director in January 2007, and then resigned from his position as legal counsel, effective April 1, 2007. He was replaced by <a href="/wiki/Mike_Godwin" title="Mike Godwin">Mike Godwin</a>, who served as general counsel and legal coordinator from July 2007<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88"><span>[</span>88<span>]</span></a></sup> until 2010.</p>
<p>In January 2007, Carolyn Doran was named chief operating officer and Sandy Ordonez joined as <a href="//wikimediafoundation.org/wiki/Head_of_Communications" class="extiw" title="wmf:Head of Communications">head of communications</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89"><span>[</span>89<span>]</span></a></sup> Doran began working as a part-time bookkeeper in 2006 after being sent by a <a href="/wiki/Temporary_work" title="Temporary work">temporary agency</a>. Doran later left the foundation in July 2007, and <a href="/wiki/Sue_Gardner" title="Sue Gardner">Sue Gardner</a> was hired as consultant and special advisor (later CEO). Her departure from the organization was cited by Florence Devouard as one of the reasons the foundation took about seven months to release its fiscal 2007 financial audit.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90"><span>[</span>90<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:149_New_Montgomery_Street,_San_Francisco.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/149_New_Montgomery_Street%2C_San_Francisco.jpg/220px-149_New_Montgomery_Street%2C_San_Francisco.jpg" width="220" height="109" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/149_New_Montgomery_Street%2C_San_Francisco.jpg/330px-149_New_Montgomery_Street%2C_San_Francisco.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/149_New_Montgomery_Street%2C_San_Francisco.jpg/440px-149_New_Montgomery_Street%2C_San_Francisco.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1731" data-file-height="860" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:149_New_Montgomery_Street,_San_Francisco.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The location of the Wikimedia Foundation's San Francisco headquarters</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Danny Wool, officially the grant coordinator but also largely involved in <a href="/wiki/Fundraising" title="Fundraising">fundraising</a> and business development, resigned in March 2007. Wales was accused by former Wikimedia Foundation employee Danny Wool of misusing the foundation's funds for recreational purposes. Wool also stated that Wales had his Wikimedia credit card taken away in part because of his spending habits, a claim Wales denied.<sup id="cite_ref-Moses_91-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Moses-91"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup> In February 2007, the foundation added a new position, chapters coordinator, and hired Delphine Ménard,<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92"><span>[</span>92<span>]</span></a></sup> who had been occupying the position as a volunteer since August 2005. Cary Bass was hired in March 2007 in the position of volunteer coordinator. Oleta McHenry was brought in as accountant in May 2007, through a temporary placement agency and made the official full-time accountant in August 2007. In January 2008, the foundation appointed Veronique Kessler as the new chief financial and operating officer, Kul Wadhwa as head of business development, and Jay Walsh as head of communications.</p>
<p>By early 2015, the foundation had well over 200 employees.</p>
<p>According to <i>Business Insider</i>, "In September of 2012, there was a quite a bit of media attention surrounding two Wikipedia employees who were running a PR business on the side and editing Wikipedia on behalf of their clients."<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93"><span>[</span>93<span>]</span></a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template noprint Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTRS" title="Wikipedia:NOTRS" class="mw-redirect"><span title="Doesn't seem like the strongest source for these claims, particularly about BLPs (February 2014)">better&#160;source&#160;needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Disputes_and_lawsuits">Disputes and lawsuits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Disputes and lawsuits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Post-Sopa_Blackout_Party_for_Wikimedia_Foundation_staff-3.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Post-Sopa_Blackout_Party_for_Wikimedia_Foundation_staff-3.jpg/220px-Post-Sopa_Blackout_Party_for_Wikimedia_Foundation_staff-3.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Post-Sopa_Blackout_Party_for_Wikimedia_Foundation_staff-3.jpg/330px-Post-Sopa_Blackout_Party_for_Wikimedia_Foundation_staff-3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/Post-Sopa_Blackout_Party_for_Wikimedia_Foundation_staff-3.jpg/440px-Post-Sopa_Blackout_Party_for_Wikimedia_Foundation_staff-3.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5184" data-file-height="3456" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Post-Sopa_Blackout_Party_for_Wikimedia_Foundation_staff-3.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Wikimedia Foundation post-<a href="/wiki/Stop_Online_Piracy_Act" title="Stop Online Piracy Act">SOPA</a> party, 2012</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_litigation_involving_the_Wikimedia_Foundation" title="List of litigation involving the Wikimedia Foundation" class="mw-redirect">List of litigation involving the Wikimedia Foundation</a></div>
<table class="metadata plainlinks ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">
<tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg" class="image"><img alt="[icon]" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" width="20" height="14" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="44" data-file-height="31" /></a></td>
<td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">This section requires <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;action=edit">expansion</a>. <small><i>(January 2010)</i></small></span></td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>Many disputes have resulted in <a href="/wiki/Litigation" title="Litigation" class="mw-redirect">litigation</a><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94"><span>[</span>94<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95"><span>[</span>95<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96"><span>[</span>96<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97"><span>[</span>97<span>]</span></a></sup> while others have not.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98"><span>[</span>98<span>]</span></a></sup> Attorney Matt Zimmerman stated, "Without strong liability protection, it would be difficult for Wikipedia to continue to provide a platform for user-created encyclopedia content."<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99"><span>[</span>99<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In December 2011, the Foundation hired Washington, DC lobbyist <a href="/wiki/Dow_Lohnes" title="Dow Lohnes">Dow Lohnes</a> Government Strategies LLC to lobby the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">United States Congress</a> with regard to "Civil Rights/Civil Liberties" and "Copyright/Patent/Trademark."<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100"><span>[</span>100<span>]</span></a></sup> At the time of the hire the Foundation was concerned specifically about a bill known as the <a href="/wiki/Stop_Online_Piracy_Act" title="Stop Online Piracy Act">Stop Online Piracy Act</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101"><span>[</span>101<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In October 2013, a German Court ruled that the Wikimedia Foundation can be held liable for content added to Wikipedia.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102"><span>[</span>102<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In June 2014, a copyright infringement lawsuit was filed by Bildkonst Upphovsrätt i Sverige against Wikimedia Sweden.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103"><span>[</span>103<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On June 20, 2014, a defamation lawsuit (Law Division civil case No. L-1400-14) involving Wikipedia editors was filed with the Mercer County Superior Court in New Jersey seeking, inter alia, compensatory and punitive damages.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104"><span>[</span>104<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105"><span>[</span>105<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In a March 10, 2015, op-ed for <i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i>, Wales and Tretikov announced the Foundation was filing <a href="/wiki/ACLU_and_others_v._NSA" title="ACLU and others v. NSA" class="mw-redirect">a lawsuit</a> against the <a href="/wiki/National_Security_Agency" title="National Security Agency">National Security Agency</a>, calling into question its practice of <a href="/wiki/Mass_surveillance" title="Mass surveillance">mass surveillance</a>, which they argued infringed the constitutional rights of the Foundation's readers, editors and staff.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106"><span>[</span>106<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107"><span>[</span>107<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-rayman_108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rayman-108"><span>[</span>108<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
